### USER - 2025-12-30 01:40:20

which of these apps can I safely delete?

---

### GEMINI - 2025-12-30 01:40:46

Deciding what is "safe" to delete depends on what you use, but we can categorize these into **User Apps** (safe to remove) and **System Components** (risky to remove).

Since you are running **CachyOS (Arch-based)** with both **KDE Plasma** and **COSMIC** desktop environments, you have a lot of overlapping system tools.

### 1. Completely Safe to Delete (User Applications)
Removing these will not affect your system's stability.
*   **Games:** `Cyberpunk 2077`, `Dead Cells`, `Steam`.
*   **Web Apps/Shortcuts:** `Claude`, `Gemini`, `Fastmail`, `Gmail`, `Google Maps`, `iCloud Mail`, `YouTube`, `Helium`, `Antigravity`.
*   **Development Tools:** `VSCodium`, `Micro`, `Meld`, `Alacritty`.
*   **Media & Internet:** `mpv Media Player`, `Haruna`, `Mullvad VPN`, `Lutris`, `Winetricks`, `Protontricks`.

### 2. Safe, but Check First (Desktop Environment Apps)
You have two sets of standard applications installed. If you stick to one Desktop Environment (e.g., KDE), you *could* remove the apps from the other, but they are often useful to keep as backups.
*   **If you mainly use KDE:** You could remove `COSMIC Terminal`, `COSMIC Files`, `COSMIC Settings`, `COSMIC Store`.
*   **If you mainly use COSMIC:** You could remove `Konsole`, `Dolphin`, `Spectacle` (though KDE tools are often deeply integrated).

### 3. Do NOT Delete (System & Maintenance Tools)
These manage your hardware, updates, and settings. Removing them can break your system.
*   **CachyOS Tools:** `CachyOS Hello`, `CachyOS Kernel Manager`, `CachyOS Package Installer`.
*   **Core Management:** `Octopi`, `Btrfs Assistant`, `NVIDIA X Server Settings`, `System Monitor`, `Info Center`.
*   **System Daemons:** `Avahi`, `KDE Daemon (KDED)`, `Polkit`, `Xwayland`.

### How to remove them?
On your system, these are likely installed via `pacman` (system packages) or `flatpak`.

**To check how a specific app is installed and remove it:**
Tell me which app you want to remove (e.g., "Delete Cyberpunk"), and I can find the correct command for you.

### GEMINI - 2025-12-30 04:30:40

I will create a shell script named `toggle-theme.sh` in the `Gemini-Playground` directory. This script will toggle the system and application themes between light and dark modes, updating configurations for COSMIC, GTK, Alacritty, Antigravity, VSCodium, and KDE, and then display a notification.

**Tool Calls:**

<details>
<summary>Tool: <code>write_file</code></summary>

**Arguments:**
```json
{
  "content": "#!/bin/bash\n\n# Files\nCOSMIC_MODE_FILE=\"$HOME/.config/cosmic/com.system76.CosmicTheme.Mode/v1/is_dark\"\nALACRITTY_CONF=\"$HOME/.config/alacritty/current_theme.toml\"\nANTIGRAVITY_CONF=\"$HOME/.config/Antigravity/User/settings.json\"\nVSCODIUM_FLATPAK_CONF=\"$HOME/.var/app/com.vscodium.codium-insiders/config/VSCodium - Insiders/User/settings.json\"\n\n# Function to read COSMIC mode\nget_mode() {\n    if [ -f \"$COSMIC_MODE_FILE\" ]; then\n        cat \"$COSMIC_MODE_FILE\"\n    else\n        echo \"false\" # Default to light if missing\n    fi\n}\n\nIS_DARK=$(get_mode)\n\nif [ \"$IS_DARK\" == \"true\" ]; then\n    # Switch to LIGHT\n    echo \"Switching to Light Mode...\"\n    NEW_MODE=\"false\"\n    \n    # COSMIC\n    mkdir -p \"$(dirname \"$COSMIC_MODE_FILE\")\"\n    echo \"false\" > \"$COSMIC_MODE_FILE\"\n    \n    # GTK\n    gsettings set org.gnome.desktop.interface color-scheme 'prefer-light' 2>/dev/null\n    \n    # Alacritty\n    if [ -f \"$HOME/.config/alacritty/light.toml\" ]; then\n        cp \"$HOME/.config/alacritty/light.toml\" \"$ALACRITTY_CONF\"\n    fi\n    \n    # Antigravity (VS Code)\n    if [ -f \"$ANTIGRAVITY_CONF\" ]; then\n        tmp=$(mktemp)\n        jq '.\"workbench.colorTheme\" = \"Default Light Modern\"' \"$ANTIGRAVITY_CONF\" > \"$tmp\" && mv \"$tmp\" \"$ANTIGRAVITY_CONF\"\n    fi\n    \n    # VSCodium Flatpak\n    if [ -f \"$VSCODIUM_FLATPAK_CONF\" ]; then\n        tmp=$(mktemp)\n        jq '.\"workbench.colorTheme\" = \"Default Light Modern\"' \"$VSCODIUM_FLATPAK_CONF\" > \"$tmp\" && mv \"$tmp\" \"$VSCODIUM_FLATPAK_CONF\"\n    else\n        mkdir -p \"$(dirname \"$VSCODIUM_FLATPAK_CONF\")\"\n        echo '{\"workbench.colorTheme\": \"Default Light Modern\"}' > \"$VSCODIUM_FLATPAK_CONF\"\n    fi\n    \n    # Kate / KDE\n    if command -v kwriteconfig6 &> /dev/null; then\n        kwriteconfig6 --file kdeglobals --group General --key ColorScheme BreezeLight\n    elif command -v kwriteconfig5 &> /dev/null; then\n        kwriteconfig5 --file kdeglobals --group General --key ColorScheme BreezeLight\n    fi\n\n    # Trigger update for running KDE apps (sometimes works)\n    dbus-send --type=signal /KGlobalSettings org.kde.KGlobalSettings.notifyChange int32:0 int32:0 2>/dev/null\n    \n    notify-send -i \"$HOME/.local/share/icons/theme-toggle.svg\" \"Theme Toggled\" \"Switched to Light Mode\"\n\nelse\n    # Switch to DARK\n    echo \"Switching to Dark Mode...\"\n    NEW_MODE=\"true\"\n    \n    # COSMIC\n    mkdir -p \"$(dirname \"$COSMIC_MODE_FILE\")\"\n    echo \"true\" > \"$COSMIC_MODE_FILE\"\n    \n    # GTK\n    gsettings set org.gnome.desktop.interface color-scheme 'prefer-dark' 2>/dev/null\n    \n    # Alacritty\n    if [ -f \"$HOME/.config/alacritty/dark.toml\" ]; then\n        cp \"$HOME/.config/alacritty/dark.toml\" \"$ALACRITTY_CONF\"\n    fi\n    \n    # Antigravity\n    if [ -f \"$ANTIGRAVITY_CONF\" ]; then\n        tmp=$(mktemp)\n        jq '.\"workbench.colorTheme\" = \"Default Dark Modern\"' \"$ANTIGRAVITY_CONF\" > \"$tmp\" && mv \"$tmp\" \"$ANTIGRAVITY_CONF\"\n    fi\n    \n    # VSCodium Flatpak\n    if [ -f \"$VSCODIUM_FLATPAK_CONF\" ]; then\n        tmp=$(mktemp)\n        jq '.\"workbench.colorTheme\" = \"Default Dark Modern\"' \"$VSCODIUM_FLATPAK_CONF\" > \"$tmp\" && mv \"$tmp\" \"$VSCODIUM_FLATPAK_CONF\"\n    else\n        mkdir -p \"$(dirname \"$VSCODIUM_FLATPAK_CONF\")\"\n        echo '{\"workbench.colorTheme\": \"Default Dark Modern\"}' > \"$VSCODIUM_FLATPAK_CONF\"\n    fi\n    \n    # Kate / KDE\n    if command -v kwriteconfig6 &> /dev/null; then\n        kwriteconfig6 --file kdeglobals --group General --key ColorScheme BreezeDark\n    elif command -v kwriteconfig5 &> /dev/null; then\n        kwriteconfig5 --file kdeglobals --group General --key ColorScheme BreezeDark\n    fi\n\n    # Trigger update for running KDE apps\n    dbus-send --type=signal /KGlobalSettings org.kde.KGlobalSettings.notifyChange int32:0 int32:0 2>/dev/null\n\n    notify-send -i \"$HOME/.local/share/icons/theme-toggle.svg\" \"Theme Toggled\" \"Switched to Dark Mode\"\nfi\n",
  "file_path": "/home/mischa/Gemini-Playground/toggle-theme.sh"
}
```

### GEMINI - 2025-12-30 04:33:24

I will overwrite the `toggle-theme` script in `~/.local/bin` with an updated version that accepts "dark" or "light" arguments to force a specific mode, in addition to its default toggling behavior.

**Tool Calls:**

<details>
<summary>Tool: <code>write_file</code></summary>

**Arguments:**
```json
{
  "file_path": "/home/mischa/.local/bin/toggle-theme",
  "content": "#!/bin/bash\n\n# Files\nCOSMIC_MODE_FILE=\"$HOME/.config/cosmic/com.system76.CosmicTheme.Mode/v1/is_dark\"\nALACRITTY_CONF=\"$HOME/.config/alacritty/current_theme.toml\"\nANTIGRAVITY_CONF=\"$HOME/.config/Antigravity/User/settings.json\"\nVSCODIUM_FLATPAK_CONF=\"$HOME/.var/app/com.vscodium.codium-insiders/config/VSCodium - Insiders/User/settings.json\"\n\n# Function to read COSMIC mode\nget_mode() {\n    if [ -f \"$COSMIC_MODE_FILE\" ]; then\n        cat \"$COSMIC_MODE_FILE\"\n    else\n        echo \"false\" # Default to light if missing\n    fi\n}\n\nCURRENT_MODE=$(get_mode)\nFORCE_MODE=\"$1\"\n\n# Determine target action\n# If \"dark\" arg passed, we want to go Dark (act as if currently Light/false)\n# If \"light\" arg passed, we want to go Light (act as if currently Dark/true)\nif [[ \"${FORCE_MODE,,}\" == \"dark\" ]]; then\n    IS_DARK_STATE=\"false\"\nelif [[ \"${FORCE_MODE,,}\" == \"light\" ]]; then\n    IS_DARK_STATE=\"true\"\nelse\n    IS_DARK_STATE=\"$CURRENT_MODE\"\nfi\n\nif [ \"$IS_DARK_STATE\" == \"true\" ]; then\n    # ==========================================\n    # Switch to LIGHT\n    # ==========================================\n    echo \"Switching to Light Mode...\"\n    NEW_MODE=\"false\"\n    \n    # COSMIC\n    mkdir -p \"$(dirname \"$COSMIC_MODE_FILE\")\"\n    echo \"false\" > \"$COSMIC_MODE_FILE\"\n    \n    # GTK\n    gsettings set org.gnome.desktop.interface color-scheme 'prefer-light' 2>/dev/null\n    \n    # Alacritty\n    if [ -f \"$HOME/.config/alacritty/light.toml\" ]; then\n        cp \"$HOME/.config/alacritty/light.toml\" \"$ALACRITTY_CONF\"\n    fi\n    \n    # Antigravity (VS Code)\n    if [ -f \"$ANTIGRAVITY_CONF\" ]; then\n        tmp=$(mktemp)\n        jq '.\"workbench.colorTheme\" = \"Default Light Modern\"' \"$ANTIGRAVITY_CONF\" > \"$tmp\" && mv \"$tmp\" \"$ANTIGRAVITY_CONF\"\n    fi\n    \n    # VSCodium Flatpak\n    if [ -f \"$VSCODIUM_FLATPAK_CONF\" ]; then\n        tmp=$(mktemp)\n        jq '.\"workbench.colorTheme\" = \"Default Light Modern\"' \"$VSCODIUM_FLATPAK_CONF\" > \"$tmp\" && mv \"$tmp\" \"$VSCODIUM_FLATPAK_CONF\"\n    else\n        mkdir -p \"$(dirname \"$VSCODIUM_FLATPAK_CONF\")\"\n        echo '{\"workbench.colorTheme\": \"Default Light Modern\"}' > \"$VSCODIUM_FLATPAK_CONF\"\n    fi\n    \n    # Kate / KDE\n    if command -v kwriteconfig6 &> /dev/null; then\n        kwriteconfig6 --file kdeglobals --group General --key ColorScheme BreezeLight\n    elif command -v kwriteconfig5 &> /dev/null; then\n        kwriteconfig5 --file kdeglobals --group General --key ColorScheme BreezeLight\n    fi\n\n    # Trigger update for running KDE apps\n    dbus-send --type=signal /KGlobalSettings org.kde.KGlobalSettings.notifyChange int32:0 int32:0 2>/dev/null\n    \n    notify-send -i \"$HOME/.local/share/icons/theme-toggle.svg\" \"Theme Toggled\" \"Switched to Light Mode\"\n\nelse\n    # ==========================================\n    # Switch to DARK\n    # ==========================================\n    echo \"Switching to Dark Mode...\"\n    NEW_MODE=\"true\"\n    \n    # COSMIC\n    mkdir -p \"$(dirname \"$COSMIC_MODE_FILE\")\"\n    echo \"true\" > \"$COSMIC_MODE_FILE\"\n    \n    # GTK\n    gsettings set org.gnome.desktop.interface color-scheme 'prefer-dark' 2>/dev/null\n    \n    # Alacritty\n    if [ -f \"$HOME/.config/alacritty/dark.toml\" ]; then\n        cp \"$HOME/.config/alacritty/dark.toml\" \"$ALACRITTY_CONF\"\n    fi\n    \n    # Antigravity\n    if [ -f \"$ANTIGRAVITY_CONF\" ]; then\n        tmp=$(mktemp)\n        jq '.\"workbench.colorTheme\" = \"Default Dark Modern\"' \"$ANTIGRAVITY_CONF\" > \"$tmp\" && mv \"$tmp\" \"$ANTIGRAVITY_CONF\"\n    fi\n    \n    # VSCodium Flatpak\n    if [ -f \"$VSCODIUM_FLATPAK_CONF\" ]; then\n        tmp=$(mktemp)\n        jq '.\"workbench.colorTheme\" = \"Default Dark Modern\"' \"$VSCODIUM_FLATPAK_CONF\" > \"$tmp\" && mv \"$tmp\" \"$VSCODIUM_FLATPAK_CONF\"\n    else\n        mkdir -p \"$(dirname \"$VSCODIUM_FLATPAK_CONF\")\"\n        echo '{\"workbench.colorTheme\": \"Default Dark Modern\"}' > \"$VSCODIUM_FLATPAK_CONF\"\n    fi\n    \n    # Kate / KDE\n    if command -v kwriteconfig6 &> /dev/null; then\n        kwriteconfig6 --file kdeglobals --group General --key ColorScheme BreezeDark\n    elif command -v kwriteconfig5 &> /dev/null; then\n        kwriteconfig5 --file kdeglobals --group General --key ColorScheme BreezeDark\n    fi\n\n    # Trigger update for running KDE apps\n    dbus-send --type=signal /KGlobalSettings org.kde.KGlobalSettings.notifyChange int32:0 int32:0 2>/dev/null\n\n    notify-send -i \"$HOME/.local/share/icons/theme-toggle.svg\" \"Theme Toggled\" \"Switched to Dark Mode\"\nfi\n"
}
```

### GEMINI - 2025-12-30 04:34:22

I have created a comprehensive theme toggle system for your COSMIC environment.

**Features:**
*   **One-Click Toggle:** Switches themes for **COSMIC DE, Alacritty, Antigravity, VSCodium (Flatpak), Kate, and GTK apps**.
*   **Launcher Integration:** Search for "Toggle Dark/Light Mode" in your launcher.
*   **Quick Actions:** Right-click the launcher icon to force "Switch to Dark Mode" or "Switch to Light Mode".
*   **Icon:** A minimal custom light/dark glyph.

**Files Created:**
*   `~/.local/bin/toggle-theme`: The master control script.
*   `~/.local/share/applications/toggle-theme.desktop`: Launcher entry.
*   `~/.local/share/icons/theme-toggle.svg`: Custom icon.
*   `~/.config/alacritty/`: Added `light.toml`, `dark.toml`, and configured `alacritty.toml` to dynamic imports.

**To use it:**
*   Open your launcher (Super key) and type **"Toggle"**.
*   Or run `toggle-theme` from your terminal.

### GEMINI - 2025-12-30 04:46:06

I will modify the `toggle-theme` script to explicitly update the `gtk-application-prefer-dark-theme` and `gtk-theme-name` settings in the `settings.ini` files for both GTK 3.0 and GTK 4.0. This ensures that applications like Helium, which rely on these files, correctly detect the theme change.

**Tool Calls:**

<details>
<summary>Tool: <code>replace</code></summary>

**Arguments:**
```json
{
  "instruction": "Add logic to update gtk-3.0 and gtk-4.0 settings.ini files for both Light and Dark modes. ensure that the gtk-theme-name is also updated (Breeze vs Breeze-Dark).",
  "new_string": "    # GTK\n    gsettings set org.gnome.desktop.interface color-scheme 'prefer-light' 2>/dev/null\n    \n    # Update GTK 3.0 and 4.0 config files explicitly (for apps like Helium/Chromium)\n    for gtk_dir in \"$HOME/.config/gtk-3.0\" \"$HOME/.config/gtk-4.0\"; do\n        if [ -f \"$gtk_dir/settings.ini\" ]; then\n            # Use sed to replace/add the prefer-dark-theme line\n            if grep -q \"gtk-application-prefer-dark-theme\" \"$gtk_dir/settings.ini\"; then\n                sed -i 's/gtk-application-prefer-dark-theme=.*/gtk-application-prefer-dark-theme=false/' \"$gtk_dir/settings.ini\"\n            else\n                sed -i '/\\[Settings\\]/a gtk-application-prefer-dark-theme=false' \"$gtk_dir/settings.ini\"\n            fi\n            \n            # Update theme name if present (Optional, but helps some apps)\n            sed -i 's/gtk-theme-name=.*Dark.*/gtk-theme-name=Breeze/' \"$gtk_dir/settings.ini\"\n            sed -i 's/gtk-icon-theme-name=.*-dark/gtk-icon-theme-name=breeze/' \"$gtk_dir/settings.ini\"\n        fi\n    done",
  "file_path": "/home/mischa/.local/bin/toggle-theme",
  "old_string": "    # GTK\n    gsettings set org.gnome.desktop.interface color-scheme 'prefer-light' 2>/dev/null"
}
```

**Result:**
```json
[
  {
    "functionResponse": {
      "id": "replace-1767069966098-2afdeaae186058",
      "name": "replace",
      "response": {
        "output": "Successfully modified file: /home/mischa/.local/bin/toggle-theme (1 replacements)."
      }
    }
  }
]
```
</details>

### GEMINI - 2025-12-30 04:46:14

I will apply the same GTK 3.0 and 4.0 `settings.ini` updates to the "Dark Mode" section of the `toggle-theme` script, setting `gtk-application-prefer-dark-theme` to `true` and updating the theme names to "Breeze-Dark".

**Tool Calls:**

<details>
<summary>Tool: <code>replace</code></summary>

**Arguments:**
```json
{
  "old_string": "    # GTK\n    gsettings set org.gnome.desktop.interface color-scheme 'prefer-dark' 2>/dev/null",
  "instruction": "Add the corresponding GTK config update logic to the Dark Mode section.",
  "file_path": "/home/mischa/.local/bin/toggle-theme",
  "new_string": "    # GTK\n    gsettings set org.gnome.desktop.interface color-scheme 'prefer-dark' 2>/dev/null\n    \n    # Update GTK 3.0 and 4.0 config files explicitly\n    for gtk_dir in \"$HOME/.config/gtk-3.0\" \"$HOME/.config/gtk-4.0\"; do\n        if [ -f \"$gtk_dir/settings.ini\" ]; then\n            # Use sed to replace/add the prefer-dark-theme line\n            if grep -q \"gtk-application-prefer-dark-theme\" \"$gtk_dir/settings.ini\"; then\n                sed -i 's/gtk-application-prefer-dark-theme=.*/gtk-application-prefer-dark-theme=true/' \"$gtk_dir/settings.ini\"\n            else\n                sed -i '/\\[Settings\\]/a gtk-application-prefer-dark-theme=true' \"$gtk_dir/settings.ini\"\n            fi\n            \n            # Update theme name to Dark variant\n            sed -i 's/gtk-theme-name=Breeze$/gtk-theme-name=Breeze-Dark/' \"$gtk_dir/settings.ini\"\n            sed -i 's/gtk-icon-theme-name=breeze$/gtk-icon-theme-name=breeze-dark/' \"$gtk_dir/settings.ini\"\n        fi\n    done"
}
```

```json

      "name": "replace",
      "response": {
        "output": "Successfully modified file: /home/mischa/.local/bin/toggle-theme (1 replacements)."
      }

  }
]
```

### GEMINI - 2025-12-30 04:46:27

I have updated the `toggle-theme` script to fix the issue with Helium (and other Chromium-based apps) not switching themes.

**The Fix:**
Helium uses Chromium, which on your system looks at `~/.config/gtk-3.0/settings.ini` to decide whether to render in Dark Mode or Light Mode. My previous script was only updating the GNOME settings (`gsettings`), which Helium wasn't seeing.

**What I changed:**
I modified `~/.local/bin/toggle-theme` to:
1.  **Explicitly edit** `~/.config/gtk-3.0/settings.ini` and `~/.config/gtk-4.0/settings.ini`.
2.  **Set** `gtk-application-prefer-dark-theme=true/false`.
3.  **Switch** the GTK theme name between `Breeze` and `Breeze-Dark`.

**How to verify:**
1.  Ensure your **Dark Reader** extension in Helium is set to **"Auto"** (System) mode.
    *   Click the Dark Reader icon -> Click "Auto" (if available) or ensure it's "On" and "Use system color scheme" is checked in its settings.
2.  Run the toggle again:
    *   `toggle-theme light`
    *   `toggle-theme dark`

Helium should now pick up the change instantly (or within a few seconds) without needing a restart.

### GEMINI - 2025-12-30 06:38:56

I will modify the `toggle-theme` script to specifically restart the Helium process when the theme is toggled. This is necessary because Helium (running as a specific Chromium build) does not reliably detect the GTK theme change dynamically, causing it to "blink" and revert to light mode. Restarting the process ensures it picks up the new theme settings from the updated `settings.ini` and `gsettings`.

**Tool Calls:**

<details>
<summary>Tool: <code>replace</code></summary>

**Arguments:**
```json
{
  "new_string": "    # Kate / KDE\n    if command -v kwriteconfig6 &> /dev/null; then\n        kwriteconfig6 --file kdeglobals --group General --key ColorScheme BreezeLight\n    elif command -v kwriteconfig5 &> /dev/null; then\n        kwriteconfig5 --file kdeglobals --group General --key ColorScheme BreezeLight\n    fi\n\n    # Trigger update for running KDE apps (sometimes works)\n    dbus-send --type=signal /KGlobalSettings org.kde.KGlobalSettings.notifyChange int32:0 int32:0 2>/dev/null\n    \n    # Restart Helium if running to force theme update\n    if pgrep -x \"helium\" > /dev/null; then\n        pkill -x \"helium\"\n        # Wait a moment for it to close, then restart it in background\n        sleep 1\n        nohup /home/mischa/.local/bin/helium >/dev/null 2>&1 &\n    fi\n    \n    notify-send -i \"$HOME/.local/share/icons/theme-toggle.svg\" \"Theme Toggled\" \"Switched to Light Mode\"\n\nelse\n    # ==========================================\n    # Switch to DARK\n    # ==========================================\n    echo \"Switching to Dark Mode...\"\n",
  "old_string": "    # Kate / KDE\n    if command -v kwriteconfig6 &> /dev/null; then\n        kwriteconfig6 --file kdeglobals --group General --key ColorScheme BreezeLight\n    elif command -v kwriteconfig5 &> /dev/null; then\n        kwriteconfig5 --file kdeglobals --group General --key ColorScheme BreezeLight\n    fi\n\n    # Trigger update for running KDE apps (sometimes works)\n    dbus-send --type=signal /KGlobalSettings org.kde.KGlobalSettings.notifyChange int32:0 int32:0 2>/dev/null\n    \n    notify-send -i \"$HOME/.local/share/icons/theme-toggle.svg\" \"Theme Toggled\" \"Switched to Light Mode\"\n\nelse\n    # ==========================================\n    # Switch to DARK\n    # ==========================================\n    echo \"Switching to Dark Mode...\"\n",
```

### GEMINI - 2025-12-30 06:39:30

I have updated the `toggle-theme` script to force a restart of Helium when toggling themes.

**Why this is necessary:**
Helium (Chromium) was detecting the GTK theme change but then getting overridden by its internal state or a conflict, causing the "blink" effect. By restarting the process, it launches fresh and correctly picks up the new `gtk-application-prefer-dark-theme` setting we applied to `settings.ini`.

**What happens now:**
1.  When you run `toggle-theme dark/light`.
2.  It updates all config files (COSMIC, GTK, Alacritty, Gemini, Claude).
3.  It checks if `helium` is running.
4.  If running, it closes it (`pkill helium`) and immediately restarts it (`nohup ... &`).

This should ensure Helium reliably lands on the correct theme without the flickering reversion. Try toggling it now

---

then\n        cat \"$COSMIC_MODE_FILE\"\n    else\n        echo \"false\" # Default to light if missing\n    fi\n}\n\nCURRENT_MODE=$(get_mode)\nFORCE_MODE=\"$1\"\n\n# Determine target action\n# If \"dark\" arg passed, we want to go Dark (act as if currently Light/false)\n# If \"light\" arg passed, we want to go Light (act as if currently Dark/true)\nif [[ \"${FORCE_MODE,,}\" == \"dark\" ]]; then\n    IS_DARK_STATE=\"false\"\nelif [[ \"${FORCE_MODE,,}\" == \"light\" ]]; then\n    IS_DARK_STATE=\"true\"\nelse\n    IS_DARK_STATE=\"$CURRENT_MODE\"\nfi\n\nif [ \"$IS_DARK_STATE\" == \"true\" ]; then\n    # ==========================================\n    # Switch to LIGHT\n    # ==========================================\n    echo \"Switching to Light Mode...\"\n    NEW_MODE=\"false\"\n    \n    # COSMIC\n    mkdir -p \"$(dirname \"$COSMIC_MODE_FILE\")\"\n    echo \"false\" > \"$COSMIC_MODE_FILE\"\n    \n    # GTK\n    gsettings set org.gnome.desktop.interface color-scheme 'prefer-light' 2>/dev/null\n    \n    # Update GTK 3.0 and 4.0 config files explicitly (for apps like Helium/Chromium)\n    for gtk_dir in \"$HOME/.config/gtk-3.0\" \"$HOME/.config/gtk-4.0\"; do\n        if [ -f \"$gtk_dir/settings.ini\" ]; then\n            # Use sed to replace/add the prefer-dark-theme line\n            if grep -q \"gtk-application-prefer-dark-theme\" \"$gtk_dir/settings.ini\"; then\n                sed -i 's/gtk-application-prefer-dark-theme=.*/gtk-application-prefer-dark-theme=false/' \"$gtk_dir/settings.ini\"\n            else\n                sed -i '/\\[Settings\\]/a gtk-application-prefer-dark-theme=false' \"$gtk_dir/settings.ini\"\n            fi\n            \n            # Update theme name if present (Optional, but helps some apps)\n            sed -i 's/gtk-theme-name=.*Dark.*/gtk-theme-name=Breeze/' \"$gtk_dir/settings.ini\"\n            sed -i 's/gtk-icon-theme-name=.*-dark/gtk-icon-theme-name=breeze/' \"$gtk_dir/settings.ini\"\n        fi\n    done\n    \n    # Alacritty\n    if [ -f \"$HOME/.config/alacritty/light.toml\" ]; then\n        tmp=$(mktemp)\n        jq '.\"workbench.colorTheme\" = \"Default Light Modern\"' \"$VSCODIUM_FLATPAK_CONF\" > \"$tmp\" && mv \"$tmp\" \"$VSCODIUM_FLATPAK_CONF\"\n    else\n        mkdir -p \"$(dirname \"$VSCODIUM_FLATPAK_CONF\")\"\n        echo '{\"workbench.colorTheme\": \"Default Light Modern\"}' > \"$VSCODIUM_FLATPAK_CONF\"\n    fi\n\n    # Gemini CLI\n    if [ -f \"$GEMINI_CLI_CONF\" ]; then\n        tmp=$(mktemp)\n        jq '.ui.theme = \"Default Light\"' \"$GEMINI_CLI_CONF\" > \"$tmp\" && mv \"$tmp\" \"$GEMINI_CLI_CONF\"\n    fi\n\n    # Claude Code\n    if [ -f \"$CLAUDE_CODE_CONF\" ]; then\n        tmp=$(mktemp)\n        jq '.theme = \"light-daltonized\"' \"$CLAUDE_CODE_CONF\" > \"$tmp\" && mv \"$tmp\" \"$CLAUDE_CODE_CONF\"\n    fi\n    \n    # Kate / KDE\n    if command -v kwriteconfig6 &> /dev/null; then\n        kwriteconfig6 --file kdeglobals --group General --key ColorScheme BreezeLight\n    elif command -v kwriteconfig5 &> /dev/null; then\n        kwriteconfig5 --file kdeglobals --group General --key ColorScheme BreezeLight\n    fi\n\n    # Trigger update for running KDE apps (sometimes works)\n    dbus-send --type=signal /KGlobalSettings org.kde.KGlobalSettings.notifyChange int32:0 int32:0 2>/dev/null\n    \n    # Restart Helium if running to force theme update\n    if pgrep -x \"helium\" > /dev/null; then\n        pkill -x \"helium\"\n        # Wait a moment for it to close, then restart it in background\n        sleep 1\n        nohup /home/mischa/.local/bin/helium >/dev/null 2>&1 &\n    fi\n    \n    notify-send -i \"$HOME/.local/share/icons/theme-toggle.svg\" \"Theme Toggled\" \"Switched to Light Mode\"\n\nelse\n    # ==========================================\n    # Switch to DARK\n    # ==========================================\n    echo \"Switching to Dark Mode...\"\n    NEW_MODE=\"true\"\n    \n    # COSMIC\n    mkdir -p \"$(dirname \"$COSMIC_MODE_FILE\")\"\n    echo \"true\" > \"$COSMIC_MODE_FILE\"\n    \n    # GTK\n    gsettings set org.gnome.desktop.interface color-scheme 'prefer-dark' 2>/dev/null\n    \n    # Update GTK 3.0 and 4.0 config files explicitly\n    for gtk_dir in \"$HOME/.config/gtk-3.0\" \"$HOME/.config/gtk-4.0\"; do\n        if [ -f \"$gtk_dir/settings.ini\" ]; then\n            # Use sed to replace/add the prefer-dark-theme line\n            if grep -q \"gtk-application-prefer-dark-theme\" \"$gtk_dir/settings.ini\"; then\n                sed -i 's/gtk-application-prefer-dark-theme=.*/gtk-application-prefer-dark-theme=true/' \"$gtk_dir/settings.ini\"\n            else\n                sed -i '/\\[Settings\\]/a gtk-application-prefer-dark-theme=true' \"$gtk_dir/settings.ini\"\n            fi\n            \n            # Update theme name to Dark variant\n            sed -i 's/gtk-theme-name=Breeze$/gtk-theme-name=Breeze-Dark/' \"$gtk_dir/settings.ini\"\n            sed -i 's/gtk-icon-theme-name=breeze$/gtk-icon-theme-name=breeze-dark/' \"$gtk_dir/settings.ini\"\n        fi\n    done\n    \n    # Alacritty\n    if [ -f \"$HOME/.config/alacritty/dark.toml\" ]; ### GEMINI - 2025-12-30 06:50:02

I have updated the `toggle-theme` script.

**What changed:**
1.  **Removed Restart:** Helium (and other apps) will **no longer be killed and restarted**.
2.  **Added Real-time Update:** Added `gsettings set org.gnome.desktop.interface gtk-theme 'Breeze'` (or `Breeze-Dark`). This broadcasts a signal that most Chromium-based apps (like Helium) listen to, allowing them to switch their internal "Device" theme instantly without a restart.

**Try it now:**
Run `toggle-theme dark` (or light). Helium should smoothly transition without opening a new window.
